   atha karpūraguṇāḥ //	aTa karpUra-guNAH //
   tīkṣṇoṣṇaḥ pariṇāmaśītalataraḥ kaṇḍupramehāpahaḥ	tIkzNa-uzNaH pariNAma-SItalataraH kaNxu-prameha-apahaH

   śleṣmaghnaś ca galagrahāpaharaṇaḥ saṃsuptajihvāgrajit	Slezma-GnaH ca galagraha-apaharaNaH saMsupta-jihvA-agra-jit-
   karpūraḥ khalu dīpyasaurabhaguṇaḥ pittāmayaḥ sphāṭikaḥ //	karpUraH Kalu dIpya-sOraBa-guNaH pitta-AmayaH sPAwikaH //
   galagrahe suptajihve nānā śrāva (nāsāsrāva) jalādhike /	galagrahe supta-jihve nAnA SrAvaH (nAsA-srAva) jala-aDike /
   śleṣmamehakṛmīn hanti karpūraś cākṣuṣo 'paraḥ //	Slezma-meha-kRmIn hanti karpUraH cAkzuzaH aparaH //
   pramehatṛiḍvidāhaghno lakṣmīsaubhāgyavardhanaḥ // 16 //	prameha-tRixvidAha-GnaH lakzmI-sOBAgya-varDanaH // 16 //
   atha kastūriguṇāḥ //	aTa kastUri-guNAH //
   kastūrī saurabhāḍhyā kaṭukarasayutā kṣāratiktā kaṣāyā	kastUrI sOraBa-AXyA kawuka-rasa-yutA kzAratiktA kazAyA
   śokāṭopāpahantrī kaphapavanaharā pittakṛccākṣuṣī ca /	Soka-Awopa-apahantrI kaPa-pavana-harA pitta-kRt-cAkzuzI ca /
   cittaprollāsahetur viṣamaviṣagarān gātradaurgandhyahantrī	citta-prollAsa-hetuH vizama-vizagarAn gAtra-dOrganDya-hantrI
   kṣuttṛṣṇāpittakopaṃ praśamayati bhṛśaṃ klaibyaśoṣaṃ viṣaṃ ca // 17 //	kzut-tRzNA-pitta-kopam praSamayati BRSam klEbya-Sozam vizam ca // 17 //
   athānulepanavargaḥ //	aTa-anulepana-vargaH //
   candanaṃ raktapittaghnaṃ dāhamūrchātisāranut /	candanam raktapitta-Gnam dAha-mUrCA-atisAra-nud /
   śītalaṃ śleṣmalaṃ hṛdyaṃ kiṃcid vātaprakopaṇam // 18 //	SItalam Slezmalam hRdyam kiMcid vAta-prakopaNam // 18 //
   (Ap 103)	(Ap 103)
   pittāsraṃ harate sadāhadavanaṃ vyāyādayattaḥ (?) sadā	pitta-asram harate sa-dAha-davanam vyAyAdayattaH (?) sadA

   ṛtuṣu samayayojyaṃ candanaṃ kuṅkumaṃ vā	Rtuzu samaya-yojyam candanam kuFkumam vA
   mṛgamadadhanalepaḥ sevyate sarvadaiva /	mRgamada-Dana-lepaH sevyate sarvadA-eva /

   vimaladhavalavāsaḥ sarvakālopayogyaḥ // 22 //	vimala-Dava-lavAsaH sarva-kAla-upayogyaH // 22 //

   yad vā sūtram ayaṃ vastraṃ tridoṣaśamanaṃ viduḥ // 1 //	yat vA sUtram ayam vastram tridoza-Samanam viduH // 1 //
   (Ap 104)	(Ap 104)
